<h2 class="mume-header" id="%E9%87%8D%E8%A6%81%E6%80%A7%E9%87%87%E6%A0%B7">&#x91CD;&#x8981;&#x6027;&#x91C7;&#x6837;</h2>

<p><strong>&#x5747;&#x5300;&#x534A;&#x7403;&#x91C7;&#x6837;</strong></p>
<p>&#x5728;&#x7403;&#x9762;&#x4E0A;&#x8FDB;&#x884C;&#x5747;&#x5300;&#x7684;&#x91CD;&#x8981;&#x6027;&#x91C7;&#x6837;&#x7684;&#x6982;&#x7387;&#x5BC6;&#x5EA6;&#x51FD;&#x6570;</p>
<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>d</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mrow><mn>2</mn><mi>&#x3C0;</mi></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p_d = \frac{1}{2\pi}

<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>L</mi><mi>o</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mrow><mi>N</mi><mo>&#x2217;</mo><mi>&#x3C0;</mi></mrow></mfrac><munderover><mo>&#x2211;</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><msub><mi>L</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">L_o = \frac{1}{N * \pi}\sum_{i=1}^N {L_i}

<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>f</mi><mi>s</mi></msub><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>v</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>h</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>h</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>F</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>v</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>h</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mn>90</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>v</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>h</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mrow><mn>4</mn><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>&gt;</mo><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">f_s(l,v,h,a) = \frac{D(n, h,a)F(v, h, F_0, F_{90})G(l,v,h,a)}{4 &lt;n \cdot v&gt; &lt;n \cdot l&gt;}
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord"><span <h2 class="mume-header" id="%E6%B3%95%E5%90%91%E5%88%86%E5%B8%83%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0normal-distribution-function">&#x6CD5;&#x5411;&#x5206;&#x5E03;&#x51FD;&#x6570;(Normal Distribution Function )</h2>

<p>&#x6CD5;&#x5411;&#x5206;&#x5E03;&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x8868;&#x793A;&#x7269;&#x4F53;&#x5FAE;&#x8868;&#x9762;&#x7684;&#x6CD5;&#x7EBF;&#x65B9;&#x5411;&#x7684;&#x6982;&#x7387;&#x5206;&#x5E03;&#x3002;<br>
&#x5177;&#x4F53;&#x7684;&#xFF0C;&#x4F7F;&#x7528;GGX&#x6CD5;&#x5411;&#x5206;&#x5E03;&#x51FD;&#x6570;</p>

<h2 class="mume-header" id="%E8%8F%B2%E6%B6%85%E5%B0%94%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0">&#x83F2;&#x6D85;&#x5C14;&#x51FD;&#x6570;</h2>

<p>&#x83F2;&#x6D85;&#x5C14;&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x63CF;&#x8FF0;&#x5165;&#x5C04;&#x5149;&#x7167;&#x5C04;&#x5230;&#x7269;&#x4F53;&#x5E73;&#x9762;&#x540E;&#x53CD;&#x5C04;&#x5149;&#x548C;&#x6298;&#x5C04;&#x5149;&#x7684;&#x6BD4;&#x4F8B;&#xFF0C;&#x662F;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;rgb&#x4E09;&#x7EF4;&#x7684;&#x503C;&#x3002;<br>

<h2 class="mume-header" id="%E5%87%A0%E4%BD%95%E9%98%B4%E5%BD%B1%E5%87%BD%E6%95%B0">&#x51E0;&#x4F55;&#x9634;&#x5F71;&#x51FD;&#x6570;</h2>

<p>Height-Correlated Smith Geometric Shaow Function [Heitz14]</p>
<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>G</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>v</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>l</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mn>2</mn><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>&gt;</mo><mo>+</mo><msqrt><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>+</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>&#x2212;</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow></msqrt></mrow></mfrac><mfrac><mrow><mn>2</mn><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow><mrow><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>&gt;</mo><mo>+</mo><msqrt><mrow><msup><mi>a</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo>+</mo><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mn>1</mn><mo>&#x2212;</mo><msup><mi>a</mi><mn>2</mn></msup><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow></msqrt></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">G(n, v, l, a) = 
\frac{ 2 &lt;n \cdot l&gt;} {&lt;n \cdot l&gt; + \sqrt{a^2 + (1-a^2)&lt;n \cdot l&gt;} }
\frac{ 2 &lt;n \cdot v&gt;} {&lt;n \cdot v&gt; + \sqrt{a^2 + (1-a^2)&lt;n \cdot v&gt;} }
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:1em;vertical-align:-0.25em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">G</span><span class="mopen">(</span><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mpunct">,</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.16666666666666666em;"></span><span <p>&#x7C97;&#x7CD9;&#x5EA6;&#x8D8A;&#x5927;&#xFF0C;&#x9AD8;&#x5149;BRDF&#x7684;&#x5F62;&#x72B6;&#x8D8A;&#x949D;&#xFF0C;&#x5982;&#x4E0B;&#x56FE;&#x6240;&#x793A;&#x3002;</p>

<h2 class="mume-header" id="ibl%E9%A2%84%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E6%96%B9%E6%A1%88">IBL&#x9884;&#x8BA1;&#x7B97;&#x65B9;&#x6848;</h2>

<h3 class="mume-header" id="split-integral-approximation">Split Integral Approximation</h3>

<p>split Integral Approximation&#xFF1A;&#x5C06;&#x6E32;&#x67D3;&#x65B9;&#x7A0B;&#x7684;&#x79EF;&#x5206;&#x8FD1;&#x4F3C;&#x62C6;&#x6210; ++&#x73AF;&#x5883;&#x56FE;&#x5149;&#x7167;&#x76F8;&#x5173;&#x7684;++ &#x4EE5;&#x53CA; ++&#x73AF;&#x5883;&#x56FE;&#x5149;&#x7167;&#x65E0;&#x5173;&#x7684;++ &#x4E24;&#x90E8;&#x5206;</p>
<p>&#x8FD9;&#x4E2A;&#x8FD1;&#x4F3C;&#x5E76;&#x6CA1;&#x6709;&#x7406;&#x8BBA;&#x4F9D;&#x636E;&#xFF0C;&#x662F;&#x4E00;&#x4E2A;&#x7ECF;&#x9A8C;&#x6027;&#x7684;&#x8FD1;&#x4F3C;&#x3002;&#x8FD9;&#x6837;&#x53EF;&#x4EE5;&#x628A;F0&#x548C;&#x73AF;&#x5883;&#x56FE;&#x8FDB;&#x884C;&#x89E3;&#x8026;&#xFF0C;&#x5BF9;&#x4E8E;F0&#x76F8;&#x5173;&#x7684;&#x9884;&#x79EF;&#x5206;&#x4E0D;&#x518D;&#x9700;&#x8981;&#x548C;&#x73AF;&#x5883;&#x56FE;&#x76F8;&#x5173;&#x8054;&#x3002;</p>

<p>&#x5177;&#x4F53;&#x5730;&#xFF0C;&#x505A;&#x79EF;&#x5206;&#x7684;&#x91CD;&#x8981;&#x6027;&#x91C7;&#x6837;&#xFF0C;&#x6982;&#x7387;&#x5BC6;&#x5EA6;&#x51FD;&#x6570;&#x4F7F;&#x7528;&#x5982;&#x4E0B;ps</p>
<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>s</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>h</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>h</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow><mrow><mn>4</mn><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>h</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p_s = \frac{ D(n, h,a) &lt;n \cdot h&gt;}{ 4&lt;v \cdot h&gt; }

<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>D</mi><mi>F</mi><mi>G</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mn>1</mn><mi>N</mi></mfrac><munderover><mo>&#x2211;</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><mi>F</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>v</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>h</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mn>0</mn></msub><mo separator="true">,</mo><msub><mi>F</mi><mn>90</mn></msub><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>V</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>v</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>h</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">DFG = \frac{1}{N} \sum_{i=1}^N F(v, h, F_0, F_{90})V(l,v,h,a)

stretchy="true">&#x23DF;</mo></munder><mrow><mi>D</mi><mi>F</mi><msub><mi>G</mi><mn>2</mn></msub></mrow></munder></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">DFG = \frac{1}{N} \sum_{i=1}^N V(l,v,h,a) (F_0 + ( F_{90} - F_0 )(1 - &lt;v \cdot h&gt;)^5

DFG = F_0  \underbrace{ \frac{1}{N} \sum_{i=1}^N (1-(1 - &lt;v \cdot h&gt;)^5)V(l,v,h,a) }_{DFG_1} +  F_{90} \underbrace{ \frac{1}{N} \sum_{i=1}^N (1 - &lt;v \cdot h&gt;)^5 V(l,v,h,a) }_{DFG_2}

<h3 class="mume-header" id="ld%E9%A2%84%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97">LD&#x9884;&#x8BA1;&#x7B97;</h3>

<p>LD&#x7684;&#x9884;&#x8BA1;&#x7B97;&#x7B97;&#x4E3B;&#x8981;&#x601D;&#x8DEF;&#x5982;&#x4E0B;&#xFF1A;</p>
<h4 class="mume-header" id="1-%E5%8E%9F%E5%A7%8Bld">1. &#x539F;&#x59CB;LD</h4>

<img src="https://raw.githubusercontent.com/lealzhan/lealzhan.github.io/master/_pictures/splitSum1.PNG" height="330" width="400">
<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>L</mi><mi>D</mi><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><msub><mo>&#x222B;</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">&#x3A9;</mi></msub><mrow><msub><mi>L</mi><mi>i</mi></msub><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>v</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow><mtext>&#x2009;</mtext><mi>d</mi><mi>l</mi></mrow><mrow><msub><mo>&#x222B;</mo><mi mathvariant="normal">&#x3A9;</mi></msub><mrow><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>v</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow><mtext>&#x2009;</mtext><mi>d</mi><mi>l</mi></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">LD = \frac{\int_\Omega { L_i D(l,v, n, a) &lt;n \cdot l&gt; } \,dl } { \int_\Omega {  D(l,v, n, a) &lt;n \cdot l&gt; } \,dl  }
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">L</span><span class="mord mathnormal" style="margin-right:0.02778em;">D</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span class="mrel">=</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span></span><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:2.6016400000000006em;vertical-align:-1.05082em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:1.5508200000000003em;"><span <p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>s</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>v</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>h</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow><mrow><mn>4</mn><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>h</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow></mfrac><mi>l</mi><mi>e</mi><mi>t</mi><mtext>&#xA0;</mtext><mi>v</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>n</mi><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>s</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mn>4</mn></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p_s = \frac{ D(l, v, n, a) &lt;n \cdot h&gt;}{ 4&lt;v \cdot h&gt; }

nulldelimiter"></span></span></span></span></span></span></p><p>&#x6709;</p>
<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>L</mi><mi>D</mi><mo>&#x2248;</mo><mfrac><mrow><munderover><mo>&#x2211;</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><mfrac><mrow><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>&gt;</mo><msub><mi>L</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>s</mi></msub></mfrac></mrow><mrow><munderover><mo>&#x2211;</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><mfrac><mrow><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>l</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>n</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>s</mi></msub></mfrac></mrow></mfrac><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><munderover><mo>&#x2211;</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>&gt;</mo><msub><mi>L</mi><mi>i</mi></msub></mrow><mrow><munderover><mo>&#x2211;</mo><mrow><mi>i</mi><mo>=</mo><mn>1</mn></mrow><mi>N</mi></munderover><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>l</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">LD  \approx \frac{ \sum_{i=1}^N \frac{D(l, n, n, a) &lt;n \cdot l&gt;{L_i}}{p_s}}
{ \sum_{i=1}^N \frac{ D(l, n, n, a) &lt;n \cdot l&gt;}{p_s}}

= \frac{\sum_{i=1}^N &lt;n \cdot l&gt;{L_i}}{\sum_{i=1}^N &lt;n \cdot l&gt;} 
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.68333em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord <h4 class="mume-header" id="4-%E5%AE%9E%E6%97%B6%E6%B8%B2%E6%9F%93%E6%97%B6%E8%8E%B7%E5%8F%96%E9%A2%84%E8%AE%A1%E7%AE%97%E7%BB%93%E6%9E%9C">4. &#x5B9E;&#x65F6;&#x6E32;&#x67D3;&#x65F6;&#x83B7;&#x53D6;&#x9884;&#x8BA1;&#x7B97;&#x7ED3;&#x679C;</h4>

<p>&#x5728;&#x5B9E;&#x65F6;&#x6E32;&#x67D3;&#x8FC7;&#x7A0B;&#x4E2D;&#xFF0C;&#x901A;&#x8FC7;&#x8BA1;&#x7B97;&#x89C6;&#x89D2;&#x5411;&#x91CF;v&#x7684;&#x53CD;&#x5C04;&#x5411;&#x91CF;r&#xFF0C;&#x6839;&#x636E;&#x5F53;&#x524D;&#x7684;&#x7C97;&#x7CD9;&#x5EA6;&#xFF0C;&#x53BB;&#x8303;&#x56F4;&#x9884;&#x8BA1;&#x7B97;&#x7684;&#x73AF;&#x5883;&#x56FE;&#x5F97;&#x5230;LD&#x7684;&#x503C;&#x3002;</p>
<h2 class="mume-header" id="%E9%87%8D%E8%A6%81%E6%80%A7%E9%87%87%E6%A0%B7-1">&#x91CD;&#x8981;&#x6027;&#x91C7;&#x6837;</h2>

<p>&#x5728;&#x5177;&#x4F53;&#x4F7F;&#x7528;&#x65F6;&#xFF0C;pdf&#x662F;GGX NDF*Jacobian()</p>
<p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>s</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>h</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>n</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>h</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow><mrow><mn>4</mn><mo>&lt;</mo><mi>v</mi><mo>&#x22C5;</mo><mi>h</mi><mo>&gt;</mo></mrow></mfrac><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mtext>&#x5047;&#x8BBE;</mtext><mi>n</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>v</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><msub><mi>p</mi><mi>s</mi></msub><mo>=</mo><mfrac><mrow><mi>D</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>h</mi><mo separator="true">,</mo><mi>a</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo></mrow><mn>4</mn></mfrac></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">p_s = \frac{ D(h,a) &lt;n \cdot h&gt;}{ 4&lt;v \cdot h&gt; }
\\&#x5047;&#x8BBE;n = v,\\
p_s = \frac{ D(h,a)}{ 4 } 
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.625em;vertical-align:-0.19444em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mord mathnormal">p</span><span class="msupsub"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.151392em;"><span mtight">s</span></span></span></span><span class="vlist-s">&#x200B;</span></span><span class="vlist-r"><span class="vlist" style="height:0.15em;"><span></span></span></span></span></span></span><span class="strut" style="height:2.1521em;vertical-align:-0.7251000000000001em;"></span><span class="mord"><span class="mopen nulldelimiter"></span><span class="mfrac"><span class="vlist-t vlist-t2"><span class="mord mathnormal">n</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mbin">&#x22C5;</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2222222222222222em;"></span><span class="mord mathnormal">h</span><span class="mspace" style="margin-right:0.2777777777777778em;"></span><span <p><span class="katex-display"><span class="katex"><span class="katex-mathml"><math xmlns="http://www.w3.org/1998/Math/MathML" display="block"><semantics><mrow><mi>x</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>s</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>n</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>&#x3B8;</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>c</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>s</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>&#x3D5;</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mi>y</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>s</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>n</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>&#x3B8;</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mi>s</mi><mi>i</mi><mi>n</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>&#x3D5;</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace><mi>z</mi><mo>=</mo><mi>c</mi><mi>o</mi><mi>s</mi><mo stretchy="false">(</mo><mi>&#x3B8;</mi><mo stretchy="false">)</mo><mspace linebreak="newline"></mspace></mrow><annotation encoding="application/x-tex">x = sin(\theta)cos(\phi)\\
y = sin(\theta)sin(\phi)\\
z = cos(\theta)\\
</annotation></semantics></math></span><span class="katex-html" aria-hidden="true"><span class="base"><span class="strut" style="height:0.43056em;vertical-align:0em;"></span><span class="mord class="mume-header" id="filtered-importance-sampling">Filtered Importance Sampling</h1>

<p>&#x57FA;&#x4E8E;&#x4E0A;&#x8FF0;&#x7684;&#x91CD;&#x8981;&#x6027;&#x91C7;&#x6837;&#x65B9;&#x6CD5;&#x8FDB;&#x884C;&#x6E32;&#x67D3;&#x65B9;&#x7A0B;&#x7684;&#x79EF;&#x5206;&#x8BA1;&#x7B97;&#x4F9D;&#x7136;&#x5341;&#x5206;&#x8017;&#x65F6;&#xFF0C;Colbert&#x7B49;[Colbert 2007]&#x63D0;&#x51FA;&#x4E86;Filtered Importance Sampling&#x3002;&#x5176;&#x6838;&#x5FC3;&#x60F3;&#x6CD5;&#x662F;&#xFF0C;&#x5728;&#x505A;&#x91CD;&#x8981;&#x6027;&#x91C7;&#x6837;&#x65F6;&#xFF0C;pdf&#x8D8A;&#x5C0F;&#x7684;&#x6837;&#x672C;&#xFF0C;&#x91C7;&#x96C6;&#x73AF;&#x5883;&#x56FE;&#x7684;&#x5C42;&#x7EA7;&#x8D8A;&#x9AD8;&#x3002;&#x8FD9;&#x6837;&#x91CD;&#x8981;&#x6027;&#x91C7;&#x6837;&#x6536;&#x655B;&#x7684;&#x66F4;&#x5FEB;&#x3002;</p>
<p>&#x7531;&#x4E0B;&#x56FE;&#x53EF;&#x4EE5;&#x770B;&#x51FA;&#xFF0C;(a) Filter Importance Samping &#x6BD4; Environment Importance Sampling&#x7684;RMS&#x6536;&#x655B;&#x7684;&#x66F4;&#x5FEB;&#x3002;(b) &#x5728;&#x9AD8;&#x9891;BRDF, Filter Importance Samping&#x7684;RMS&#x8BEF;&#x5DEE;&#x548C;&#x89C6;&#x89C9;&#x6548;&#x679C;&#x90FD;&#x66F4;&#x597D;&#xFF1B;&#x5728;&#x4F4E;&#x9891;BRDF, Filter Importance Samping&#x7684;RMS&#x8BEF;&#x5DEE;&#x66F4;&#x5C0F;&#xFF0C;&#x4F46;&#x662F;&#x89C6;&#x89C9;&#x6548;&#x679C;&#x4E0D;&#x5982;Environment Importance Sampling&#x3002;</p>
